Analysis\u003c/h4\u003e\u003ca id=\"user-content-advanced-analysis\" class=\"anchor\" aria-label=\"Permalink: Advanced Analysis\" href=\"#advanced-analysis\"\u003e\u003csvg class=\"octicon octicon-link\" viewBox=\"0 0 16 16\" version=\"1.1\" width=\"16\" height=\"16\" aria-hidden=\"true\"\u003e\u003cpath d=\"m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z\"\u003e\u003c/path\u003e\u003c/svg\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e1. Strict Style\u003c/strong\u003e\nResearch suggests that broad, descriptive codebase summaries can sometimes distract LLMs and drive up token costs. The strict style combats this by giving the agent \u003cem\u003eonly\u003c/em\u003e what it can't easily \u003ccode\u003egrep\u003c/code\u003e for itself: strict constraints, undocumented quirks, and things it must \u003cem\u003enever\u003c/em\u003e do.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"uv run autogenerateagentsmd --github-repository https://github.com/pallets/flask --style strict\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003euv run autogenerateagentsmd --github-repository https://github.com/pallets/flask --style strict\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e2. Analyze Git History\u003c/strong\u003e\nAutomatically deduce anti-patterns from recently reverted commits. This powerful feature uses \u003ccode\u003egit log --grep=revert\u003c/code\u003e to inspect reverted commits in the repository (by default, looking back through the last 500 commits). It presents an \u003cstrong\u003einteractive prompt\u003c/strong\u003e where you can select exactly which reverting commits you want to analyze (e.g. \u003ccode\u003e1,2,3\u003c/code\u003e or \u003ccode\u003e1-5\u003c/code\u003e). It then feeds the diff patches of those selected commits into a dedicated DSPy module to extract explicit \"Lessons Learned\" and \"Anti-Patterns\", ensuring your AI agent avoids making the exact same mistakes previous human developers made.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"# Works on both local and cloned GitHub repositories (defaults to scanning 500 commits)\nuv run autogenerateagentsmd /path/to/local/repo --analyze-git-history\n\n# Specify a custom limit for how far back to look for reverted commits (e.g., 1000)\nuv run autogenerateagentsmd --github-repository https://github.com/pallets/flask --style strict --analyze-git-history 1000\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e Works on both local and cloned GitHub repositories (defaults to scanning 500 commits)\u003c/span\u003e\nuv run autogenerateagentsmd /path/to/local/repo --analyze-git-history\n\n\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c\"\u003e#\u003c/span\u003e Specify a custom limit for how far back to look for reverted commits (e.g., 1000)\u003c/span\u003e\nuv run autogenerateagentsmd --github-repository https://github.com/pallets/flask --style strict --analyze-git-history 1000\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch3 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e4. data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">рҹӨ– GenerateAgents.md</h1><a id="user-content--generateagentsmd" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: рҹӨ– GenerateAgents.md" href="#-generateagentsmd"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Automatically generate Agents.md for any GitHub / Local Repository. Long context enabled using dspy.RLM aka Recursive Language Models.</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">GenerateAgents.md analyzes local or GitHub repositories using Recursive Language Models (dspy.RLM) to produce optimized AGENTS.md files. It features deep codebase exploration, Git history-based anti-pattern deduction, and multiple output styles (Strict vs. Comprehensive). Powered by LiteLLM, it supports <strong>over 100+ LLM providers</strong> (Gemini, Anthropic, OpenAI, Ollama, OpenRouter, etc.) out of the box.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">рҹҡҖ Quick Start</h2><a id="user-content--quick-start" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: рҹҡҖ Quick Start" href="#-quick-start"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Clone &amp; Install</h3><a id="user-content-1-clone--install" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. Clone &amp; Install" href="#1-clone--install"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="git clone https://github.com/originalankur/GenerateAgents.md
cd GenerateAgents.md
uv sync --extra dev     # installs all deps + dev tools in one step"><pre>git clone https://github.com/originalankur/GenerateAgents.md
<span class="pl-c1">cd</span> GenerateAgents.md
uv sync --extra dev     <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> installs all deps + dev tools in one step</span></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">рҹ’Ў Don't have <code>uv</code>? Install it with <code>curl -LsSf https://astral.sh/uv/install.sh | sh</code> or see <a href="https://docs.astral.sh/uv/" rel="nofollow">uv docs</a>.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">2. Set Your API Key</h3><a id="user-content-2-set-your-api-key" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 2. Set Your API Key" href="#2-set-your-api-key"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Copy the sample env file and fill in the key for your chosen provider:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="cp .env.sample .env"><pre>cp .env.sample .env</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><em>(Make sure the <code>.env</code> file sits directly in the root directory of the project, i.e., <code>GenerateAgents.md/.env</code>)</em></p>
<p dir="auto">You only need <strong>one</strong> provider key вҖ” whichever model you select:</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Provider</th>
<th>Env Variable</th>
<th>Get a key</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Gemini</td>
<td><code>GEMINI_API_KEY</code></td>
<td><a href="https://aistudio.google.com/apikey" rel="nofollow">Google AI Studio</a></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Anthropic</td>
<td><code>ANTHROPIC_API_KEY</code></td>
<td><a href="https://console.anthropic.com/" rel="nofollow">Anthropic Console</a></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>OpenAI</td>
<td><code>OPENAI_API_KEY</code></td>
<td><a href="https://platform.openai.com/api-keys" rel="nofollow">OpenAI Platform</a></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto"><em>Note: You can use <strong>any</strong> of the 100+ providers supported by <a href="https://docs.litellm.ai/docs/providers" rel="nofollow">LiteLLM</a> (e.g., <code>OLLAMA_API_BASE</code>, <code>OPENROUTER_API_KEY</code>) simply by exposing the environment variables LiteLLM expects.</em></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">3. Run</h3><a id="user-content-3-run" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 3. Run" href="#3-run"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Default вҖ” generates AGENTS.md for a local repository (Gemini 2.5 Pro)
uv run autogenerateagentsmd /path/to/local/repo

# Analyze a public github repository using the flag
uv run autogenerateagentsmd --github-repository https://github.com/pallets/flask"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Default вҖ” generates AGENTS.md for a local repository (Gemini 2.5 Pro)</span>
uv run autogenerateagentsmd /path/to/local/repo

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Analyze a public github repository using the flag</span>
uv run autogenerateagentsmd --github-repository https://github.com/pallets/flask</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Using Specific Models</h4><a id="user-content-using-specific-models" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Using Specific Models" href="#using-specific-models"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Choose a specific model (supports ANY model natively supported by LiteLLM)
uv run autogenerateagentsmd /path/to/local/repo --model anthropic/claude-sonnet-4.6
uv run autogenerateagentsmd --github-repository https://github.com/pallets/flask --model openai/gpt-5.2
uv run autogenerateagentsmd /path/to/local/repo --model ollama/llama3

# Connect to a local provider (like Ollama or vLLM) using custom endpoints: `ollama run llama3.2:1b`
uv run autogenerateagentsmd /path/to/local/repo --model ollama_chat/llama3.2 --api-base &quot;http://localhost:11434&quot; --api-key &quot;optional-key&quot;

# Pass just a default catalog provider name (gemini, anthropic, openai)
uv run autogenerateagentsmd /path/to/local/repo --model anthropic

# List all supported catalog models
uv run autogenerateagentsmd --list-models"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Choose a specific model (supports ANY model natively supported by LiteLLM)</span>
uv run autogenerateagentsmd /path/to/local/repo --model anthropic/claude-sonnet-4.6
uv run autogenerateagentsmd --github-repository https://github.com/pallets/flask --model openai/gpt-5.2
uv run autogenerateagentsmd /path/to/local/repo --model ollama/llama3

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Connect to a local provider (like Ollama or vLLM) using custom endpoints: `ollama run llama3.2:1b`</span>
uv run autogenerateagentsmd /path/to/local/repo --model ollama_chat/llama3.2 --api-base <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>http://localhost:11434<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> --api-key <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>optional-key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Pass just a default catalog provider name (gemini, anthropic, openai)</span>
uv run autogenerateagentsmd /path/to/local/repo --model anthropic

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> List all supported catalog models</span>
uv run autogenerateagentsmd --list-models</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Advanced Analysis</h4><a id="user-content-advanced-analysis" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Advanced Analysis" href="#advanced-analysis"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>1. Strict Style</strong>
Research suggests that broad, descriptive codebase summaries can sometimes distract LLMs and drive up token costs. The strict style combats this by giving the agent <em>only</em> what it can't easily <code>grep</code> for itself: strict constraints, undocumented quirks, and things it must <em>never</em> do.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="uv run autogenerateagentsmd --github-repository https://github.com/pallets/flask --style strict"><pre>uv run autogenerateagentsmd --github-repository https://github.com/pallets/flask --style strict</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>2. Analyze Git History</strong>
Automatically deduce anti-patterns from recently reverted commits. This powerful feature uses <code>git log --grep=revert</code> to inspect reverted commits in the repository (by default, looking back through the last 500 commits). It presents an <strong>interactive prompt</strong> where you can select exactly which reverting commits you want to analyze (e.g. <code>1,2,3</code> or <code>1-5</code>). It then feeds the diff patches of those selected commits into a dedicated DSPy module to extract explicit "Lessons Learned" and "Anti-Patterns", ensuring your AI agent avoids making the exact same mistakes previous human developers made.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Works on both local and cloned GitHub repositories (defaults to scanning 500 commits)
uv run autogenerateagentsmd /path/to/local/repo --analyze-git-history

# Specify a custom limit for how far back to look for reverted commits (e.g., 1000)
uv run autogenerateagentsmd --github-repository https://github.com/pallets/flask --style strict --analyze-git-history 1000"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Works on both local and cloned GitHub repositories (defaults to scanning 500 commits)</span>
uv run autogenerateagentsmd /path/to/local/repo --analyze-git-history

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Specify a custom limit for how far back to look for reverted commits (e.g., 1000)</span>
uv run autogenerateagentsmd --github-repository https://github.com/pallets/flask --style strict --analyze-git-history 1000</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4. Find Your Output</h3><a id="user-content-4-find-your-output" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4. Find Your Output" href="#4-find-your-output"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The generated file will be saved under the <code>projects/</code> directory using the repository name.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Output Styles</h2><a id="user-content-output-styles" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Output Styles" href="#output-styles"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">GenerateAgents supports two distinct styles for <code>AGENTS.md</code>, each tailored to different AI agent setups. You can toggle between them using the <code>--style</code> flag.</p>
<p dir="auto">Here are two examples generated for the <code>flask</code> repository:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong><a href="/originalankur/GenerateAgents.md/blob/main/projects/flask/AGENTS_strict.md">Strict Style Example</a></strong> (<code>--style strict</code>) - Focuses purely on coding constraints, anti-patterns, and repository quirks.</li>
<li><strong><a href="/originalankur/GenerateAgents.md/blob/main/projects/flask/AGENTS_comprehensive.md">Comprehensive Style Example</a></strong> (<code>--style comprehensive</code>) - Includes high-level architectural overviews and explanations alongside constraints.</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h5 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">1. Comprehensive Style (Default)</h5><a id="user-content-1-comprehensive-style-default" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 1. Comprehensive Style (Default)" href="#1-comprehensive-style-default"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This builds a detailed, expansive guide. It extracts high-level abstractions like project architecture, directory mappings, data flow principles, and agent personas. Great for giving a brand-new AI agent a complete tour of the repository.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Output Format:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-md notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# AGENTS.md вҖ” &lt;repo-name&gt;

<p dir="auto">Research suggests that broad, descriptive codebase summaries can sometimes distract LLMs and drive up token costs. The strict style combats this by giving the agent <em>only</em> what it can't easily <code>grep</code> for itself: strict constraints, undocumented quirks, and things it must <em>never</em> do.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Developer Notes</h2><a id="user-content-developer-notes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Developer Notes" href="#developer-notes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">вңЁ How It Works</h3><a id="user-content--how-it-works" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: вңЁ How It Works" href="#-how-it-works"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="в”Ңв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
в”Ӯ                     GenerateAgents Pipeline                      в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ                                                                  в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ  GitHub Repo URL                                                 в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ                                                          в”Ӯ
в”Ӯ       в–ј                                                          в”Ӯ

<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="GenerateAgents/
в”ңв”Җв”Җ src/
в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ autogenerateagentsmd/    # Core package directory
в”Ӯ       в”ңв”Җв”Җ cli.py               # CLI entry point вҖ” orchestrates the analysis pipeline
в”Ӯ       в”ңв”Җв”Җ model_config.py      # Provider registry, model catalog, and CLI argument parsing
в”Ӯ       в”ңв”Җв”Җ signatures.py        # DSPy Signatures (LM task definitions)
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ ExtractCodebaseInfo        # RLM: Extracts comprehensive codebase properties
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ CompileConventionsMarkdown # CoT: Compiles RLM output into markdown
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ ExtractAgentsSections      # CoT: Translates conventions -&gt; 17 AGENTS.md fields
в”Ӯ       в”ңв”Җв”Җ modules.py           # DSPy Modules (pipeline components)
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ CodebaseConventionExtractor  # Performs RLM extraction &amp; markdown compilation
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ AgentsMdCreator              # Splits info &amp; formats final AGENTS.md text
в”Ӯ       в””в”Җв”Җ utils.py             # Utility functions
в”Ӯ           в”ңв”Җв”Җ clone_repo()              # Shallow git clone
в”Ӯ           в”ңв”Җв”Җ load_source_tree()        # Recursively map directories to a nested dict
в”Ӯ           в”ңв”Җв”Җ compile_agents_md()       # Combines the 17 extracted fields into AGENTS.md
в”Ӯ           в””в”Җв”Җ save_agents_to_disk()     # Saves output to `projects/&lt;repo_name&gt;/`
в”ңв”Җв”Җ tests/
в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ ...                      # Pytest test suite, executing end-to-end tests
в”ңв”Җв”Җ pyproject.toml               # Project metadata, dependencies &amp; tool config
в”ңв”Җв”Җ uv.lock                      # Reproducible dependency lock file
в”ңв”Җв”Җ .env.sample                  # Template for API keys
в””в”Җв”Җ .env                         # Your API keys (not committed)"><pre lang="text" class="notranslate"><code>GenerateAgents/
в”ңв”Җв”Җ src/
в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ autogenerateagentsmd/    # Core package directory
в”Ӯ       в”ңв”Җв”Җ cli.py               # CLI entry point вҖ” orchestrates the analysis pipeline
в”Ӯ       в”ңв”Җв”Җ model_config.py      # Provider registry, model catalog, and CLI argument parsing
в”Ӯ       в”ңв”Җв”Җ signatures.py        # DSPy Signatures (LM task definitions)
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ ExtractCodebaseInfo        # RLM: Extracts comprehensive codebase properties
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ CompileConventionsMarkdown # CoT: Compiles RLM output into markdown
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ ExtractAgentsSections      # CoT: Translates conventions -&gt; 17 AGENTS.md fields
в”Ӯ       в”ңв”Җв”Җ modules.py           # DSPy Modules (pipeline components)
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в”ңв”Җв”Җ CodebaseConventionExtractor  # Performs RLM extraction &amp; markdown compilation
в”Ӯ       в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ AgentsMdCreator              # Splits info &amp; formats final AGENTS.md text
в”Ӯ       в””в”Җв”Җ utils.py             # Utility functions
в”Ӯ           в”ңв”Җв”Җ clone_repo()              # Shallow git clone
в”Ӯ           в”ңв”Җв”Җ load_source_tree()        # Recursively map directories to a nested dict
в”Ӯ           в”ңв”Җв”Җ compile_agents_md()       # Combines the 17 extracted fields into AGENTS.md
в”Ӯ           в””в”Җв”Җ save_agents_to_disk()     # Saves output to `projects/&lt;repo_name&gt;/`
в”ңв”Җв”Җ tests/
в”Ӯ   в””в”Җв”Җ ...                      # Pytest test suite, executing end-to-end tests
в”ңв”Җв”Җ pyproject.toml               # Project metadata, dependencies &amp; tool config
в”ңв”Җв”Җ uv.lock                      # Reproducible dependency lock file
в”ңв”Җв”Җ .env.sample                  # Template for API keys
в””в”Җв”Җ .env                         # Your API keys (not committed)
</code></pre></div>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Environment Variables</h3><a id="user-content-environment-variables" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Environment Variables" href="#environment-variables"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">| Variable | Required | Description |
<code>|---|---|---| | </code>AUTOSKILL_MODEL<code>| No | Default model string (avoids</code>--model<code>flag) | |</code>GITHUB_REPO_URL` | No | Target repository URL (skips prompt) |</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Supported Models</h3><a id="user-content-supported-models" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Supported Models" href="#supported-models"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">GenerateAgents natively supports <strong>ANY model supported by LiteLLM</strong>!</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Important:</strong> When passing a model string to the <code>--model</code> flag, you <em>must</em> explicitly provide it in the format <code>PROVIDER/MODEL_NAME</code> (e.g., <code>ollama/llama3</code>, <code>openrouter/anthropic/claude-3-opus</code>, <code>openai/gpt-4o</code>). This ensures LiteLLM appropriately maps the request to the correct provider API. Make sure the corresponding required environment variables are exported.</p>
<p dir="auto">You can also pass custom endpoints and API keys directly via the CLI, which is especially useful for local providers:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>--api-base</code>: Allows pointing to custom local LM endpoints (e.g., <code>http://localhost:11434</code> for Ollama).</li>
<li><code>--api-key</code>: Explicitly pass an API key rather than relying on environment variables.</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">For ease of use, we maintain a "Catalog" of default fallbacks. If you just pass the provider name, these are the models we use by default:</p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Provider</th>
<th>Default Model</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Gemini</td>
<td><code>gemini/gemini-2.5-pro</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Anthropic</td>
<td><code>anthropic/claude-sonnet-4.6</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>OpenAI</td>
<td><code>openai/gpt-5.2</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto">Run <code>uv run autogenerateagentsmd --list-models</code> to view our catalog and defaults.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">рҹ§Ә Testing</h3><a id="user-content--testing" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: рҹ§Ә Testing" href="#-testing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">The project includes a robust test suite covering fast unit tests, git integration tests, and full end-to-end pipeline executions using real LLM API calls.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Test Architecture Overview</h4><a id="user-content-test-architecture-overview" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Test Architecture Overview" href="#test-architecture-overview"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="tests/
в”ңв”Җв”Җ conftest.py                    # Session-scoped fixtures (model setup, DSPy config)
в”ңв”Җв”Җ test_cli.py                    # Unit tests for CLI parsing (fully mocked)
в”ңв”Җв”Җ test_model_config.py           # Unit tests for model configuration &amp; catalog
в”ңв”Җв”Җ test_utils.py                  # Unit tests for utility functions
в”ңв”Җв”Җ test_modules.py                # Unit tests for DSPy module initialization
в”ңв”Җв”Җ test_analyze_git_history.py    # Integration tests using a temporary local git repo
в”ңв”Җв”Җ test_e2e_pipeline.py           # Full end-to-end pipeline tests (real API calls)
в””в”Җв”Җ output/                        # Persistent output from E2E test runs (ignored in git)"><pre lang="text" class="notranslate"><code>tests/
в”ңв”Җв”Җ conftest.py                    # Session-scoped fixtures (model setup, DSPy config)
в”ңв”Җв”Җ test_cli.py                    # Unit tests for CLI parsing (fully mocked)
в”ңв”Җв”Җ test_model_config.py           # Unit tests for model configuration &amp; catalog

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h4 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Running Tests</h4><a id="user-content-running-tests" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Running Tests" href="#running-tests"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Tests use <code>pytest</code>. The end-to-end tests require a valid API key configured in <code>.env</code> and internet access, as they clone real GitHub repositories and make real LLM calls. The E2E tests are marked with <code>@pytest.mark.e2e</code>.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Run ALL tests (unit, integration, and E2E)
uv run pytest tests/ -v -s

# Run ONLY E2E tests
uv run pytest tests/ -v -s -m e2e

# Run only unit/integration tests (fast, no API hits required)
uv run pytest tests/ -v -s -m &quot;not e2e&quot;

# Test with a specific LLM provider for E2E
AUTOSKILL_MODEL=openai/gpt-5.2 uv run pytest tests/ -v -s -m e2e

# Run tests filtering by a specific keyword
uv run pytest tests/ -v -s -k &quot;test_clone&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Run ALL tests (unit, integration, and E2E)</span>
uv run pytest tests/ -v -s

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Run ONLY E2E tests</span>
uv run pytest tests/ -v -s -m e2e

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Run only unit/integration tests (fast, no API hits required)</span>
uv run pytest tests/ -v -s -m <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>not e2e<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Test with a specific LLM provider for E2E</span>
AUTOSKILL_MODEL=openai/gpt-5.2 uv run pytest tests/ -v -s -m e2e

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Run tests filtering by a specific keyword</span>
uv run pytest tests/ -v -s -k <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>test_clone<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="warning">вҡ пёҸ</g-emoji> <strong>Note:</strong> E2E pipeline tests make real LLM API calls and may take 1-2 minutes per test. Test generated <code>AGENTS.md</code> and markdown outputs are persisted in <code>tests/output/&lt;repo_name&gt;/</code> for manual inspection.</p>
</blockquote>
